</header><div class="entry-content"><input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/><p><img alt="Three BBQ Black Bean Burgers served on buns with red bell pepper, cabbage, and lettuce" class="aligncenter wp-image-30686 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-7.jpg" data-pin-description="AMAZING BBQ Black Bean Burgers! 10 wholesome ingredients, BIG flavor, so satisfying #vegan #glutenfree #burger #plantbased #recipe #minimalistbaker" data-pin-media="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/MB-Smoky-Black-Bean-Burgers-Pinterest.jpg" data-pin-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-7.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-7.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-7-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-7-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-7-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-7-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-7-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>Say hello to your new favorite veggie burger.</p>
<p>It’s gluten-free, BIG on flavor, infused with smoky BBQ flavor, and perfect on the grill or stovetop. Let’s do this!</p>
<p><img alt="Display of ingredients for vegan BBQ Black Bean Burgers including mushrooms, sweet potato, pecans, black beans, BBQ sauce, coconut aminos, spices, and quinoa" class="aligncenter wp-image-30690 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker.jpg" data-pin-description="AMAZING BBQ Black Bean Burgers! 10 wholesome ingredients, BIG flavor, so satisfying #vegan #glutenfree #burger #plantbased #recipe #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/><span id="more-30802"></span></p>
<p>This burger is easy to make, requiring simple methods and <strong>10 wholesome ingredients</strong> you likely have on hand right now.</p>
<p>It all starts with black beans that are cooked down until dry and cracked, which helps keep the burgers from being mushy. Then comes toasted pecans, which are pulsed into a meal.</p>
<p><iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Dgq-LJV0_ro" width="680"></iframe><br/>
<img alt="Black beans and pecans in the food processor ready to be pulsed for BBQ Black Bean Burgers" class="aligncenter wp-image-30681 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-2.jpg" data-pin-description="AMAZING BBQ Black Bean Burgers! 10 wholesome ingredients, BIG flavor, so satisfying #vegan #glutenfree #burger #plantbased #recipe #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" height="2219" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-2.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-2.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-2-600x914.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-2-197x300.jpg 197w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-2-768x1170.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-2-672x1024.jpg 672w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-2-680x1036.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>Then we add quinoa, mushrooms, sweet potatoes, cumin, chili powder, BBQ sauce, and salt. Quinoa adds moisture and also binds the burgers, and the rest is all about flavor: sweet potatoes for sweetness, mushrooms for “meatiness” and texture, and the spices and sauce for smoky BBQ flavor.</p>
<p><img alt="All the ingredients in the food processor ready to become amazing BBQ Black Bean Burgers" class="aligncenter wp-image-30682 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-3.jpg" data-pin-description="AMAZING BBQ Black Bean Burgers! 10 wholesome ingredients, BIG flavor, so satisfying #vegan #glutenfree #burger #plantbased #recipe #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-3.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-3.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-3-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-3-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-3-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-3-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-3-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>For these burgers, it’s best to sear both sides on the stovetop and then finish baking in the oven, where they will dry out and firm up a bit. But they are firm enough for the grill as well!</p>
<p>Once cooked, it’s all about the toppings. We went for vegan buns, lettuce, cabbage, red pepper, pickles, and more BBQ + a little hot sauce. Swoon.</p>
<p><img alt="Gluten-free and vegan BBQ Black Bean Burger patties cooking in a skillet" class="aligncenter wp-image-30685 size-full" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-6.jpg" data-pin-description="AMAZING BBQ Black Bean Burgers! 10 wholesome ingredients, BIG flavor, so satisfying #vegan #glutenfree #burger #plantbased #recipe #minimalistbaker" data-pin-title="Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger" height="2184" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-6.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-6.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-6-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-6-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-6-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-6-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/AMAZING-BBQ-Black-Bean-Burgers-10-wholesome-ingredients-BIG-flavor-so-satisfying-vegan-glutenfree-burger-plantbased-recipe-minimalistbaker-6-680x1020.jpg 680w" width="1456"/></p>
<p>We hope you all LOVE these burgers! They’re:</p>
<p>Smoky<br/>
Tender<br/>
Hearty<br/>
Satisfying<br/>
Customizable<br/>
Easy to make<br/>
&amp; SO delicious</p>
<p>These burgers would make the perfect weeknight meal for you and the family or for hosting! Serve with <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/crispy-baked-garlic-matchstick-fries/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Crispy Baked Fries</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/garlicky-kale-salad-with-crispy-chickpeas/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Garlicky Kale Salad</a>, or <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/baked-plantain-chips-garlicky-guacamole/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Garlicky Guac and Plantain Chips</a>!</p>
<p>If you’re into veggie burgers, also be sure to check out our <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/sun-dried-tomato-chickpea-burgers/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Chickpea Sun-Dried Tomato Burgers</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/easy-grillable-veggie-burgers/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Grillable Veggie Burgers</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/sweet-potato-black-bean-burger/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Sweet Potato Black Bean Burger</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-black-bean-beet-burgers/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Black Bean Beet Veggie Burger</a>, <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/7-ingredient-veggie-sliders/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Simple Veggie Sliders</a>, and <a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/mexican-green-chili-veggie-burgers/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Green Chili Veggie Burger</a>.</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">Smoky BBQ Black Bean Burger</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
		Smoky, hearty black bean burgers with sweet potato, mushrooms, quinoa, and pecans. Wholesome, satisfying, BIG on flavor, and just 10 ingredients required! The ultimate veggie burgers for the grill or stovetop.	</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">

<div class="wprm-recipe-cook-time-container">

<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="34154" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> - <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="34154" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">BURGERS</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">cooked + cooled quinoa</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(<strong>divided</strong> // see notes for cooking instructions)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">15-ounce</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">can black beans</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(rinsed and dried)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2/3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">raw pecans</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">coconut or avocado oil</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(plus more for cooking burgers // or water)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">heaping cup</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sliced and peeled sweet potato </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(cut into 1/4-inch rounds)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">heaping cups</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">thinly sliced cremini or button mushrooms</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Coconut-Secret-Raw-Aminos-Pack/dp/B00CMYMRL2/?tag=minimalistbaker-20" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">coconut aminos</a></span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(<em>optional</em>)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">sea salt</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(plus more to taste)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2 1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">chili powder</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">2 1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">cumin powder</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">vegan-friendly BBQ sauce</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes"> (I like Annie’s organic original BBQ sauce // plus more for glazing)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">FOR SERVING (<em>optional</em>)</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Vegan-friendly hamburger buns OR lettuce wraps</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(and gluten-free if needed)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Veggies of choice </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(i.e. onion, cabbage, tomato, pickles)</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">If you haven’t yet, cook quinoa and set aside to cool (see notes for instructions).</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (176 C) and spread rinsed, dried black beans onto a parchment-lined baking sheet. Bake beans for 6 minutes. Then add pecans to the baking sheet and bake for 10 minutes more. The nuts should be fragrant and golden brown (be careful not to burn), and the beans should appear dry and cracked open (this way, they do not become mushy in the burger mix). Set aside to cool. Increase oven temperature to 375 degrees F (190 C).</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>In the meantime, heat a medium to large cast-iron or metal skillet over medium/medium-low heat. Once hot, add oil (or water) and the sweet potato. Cover and cook for 3-4 minutes, turning heat down if the potatoes are browning too quickly. Once browned on the underside, flip and cook for 3-4 minutes more or until tender and golden brown. Remove from the pan.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>To the still-hot pan, add the sliced mushrooms and coconut aminos (optional - sub a little salt otherwise) and cook on medium/medium-high for about 4-5 minutes, stirring frequently, or until they’re browned, fragrant, and cooked down to half their size. Set aside.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">To a food processor, add beans and pecans and blitz/pulse into a loose meal (some texture is good - you don’t want a powder).</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Next, add cooked sweet potato, mushrooms, <strong>half</strong> the quinoa, sea salt, chili powder, cumin, and BBQ sauce and pulse a few times to combine (again, some texture is good here - you're not going for a purée).</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Transfer the mixture to a mixing bowl and stir in the rest of the quinoa. Then taste and adjust flavor as needed, adding more cumin for smokiness, chili powder for heat, BBQ sauce for sweetness / depth of flavor, or salt for saltiness.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">If the mixture appears too wet, add more quinoa. If it looks too dry, add more BBQ sauce (or a little coconut aminos) to moisten.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Divide the mixture into four even balls and form into patties with your hands or by lining a 1/2 cup measuring cup with plastic wrap, packing the mixture inside, then lifting the plastic wrap out - mash slightly into more of a disc. Refrigerate burgers for 30 minutes.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Once chilled, heat the cast-iron or metal pan from earlier over medium heat. Once hot, add a bit more oil (or water) and the burgers. Cook for 4-5 minutes. Then carefully flip and cook for 4-5 minutes on the other side. Then turn off heat, glaze/brush with a bit more BBQ sauce, and transfer the pan to the oven. Bake at 375 F (190C) for 10-15 minutes more. The burgers should appear browned.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Serve as is or with toppings. We enjoyed ours on buns with butter lettuce, shredded red pepper, shredded cabbage, pickles, radish, and more BBQ sauce. Store leftovers in the refrigerator for 3-4 days or in the freezer up to 1 month.</div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-video-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header"></h3>
<iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Dgq-LJV0_ro" width="680"></iframe> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-notes-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Notes</h3>
<p>*To cook quinoa, add 1 part rinsed, drained quinoa to a small saucepan and toast for 3 minutes over medium heat. Then add 2 parts water and bring to a boil. Once boiling, cover and reduce heat to a simmer. Cook for 18 minutes or until water is absorbed. Then fluff with a fork and set off the heat uncovered to cool. (As the recipe is written, the amounts should be 1/2 cup quinoa to 1 cup water.)<br/>*Prep time does not include cooking and cooling quinoa.<br/>*Nutrition information is a rough estimate for 1 burger calculated with oil and without coconut aminos or toppings.</p>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-nutrition-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Nutrition Per Serving (1 of 4 Burgers) </h3><ul><li><strong>Calories:</strong> 289 <li><strong>Fat:</strong> 19g <li><strong>Saturated fat:</strong> 2.1g <li><strong>Sodium:</strong> 433mg <li><strong>Carbohydrates:</strong> 45.6g <li><strong>Fiber:</strong> 8.7g <li><strong>Sugar:</strong> 6.8g <li><strong>Protein:</strong> 12.4g</li></li></li></li></li></li></li></li></ul> </div>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>These burgers were so good I will never buy frozen or store bought black bean burgers ever again!<br/>
I didn’t have any issues with the burger not sticking together – we ended up not using mushrooms and left the pre made patties in the fridge for 24 hours so idk if that made a difference. Definitely my new favorite go to.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Been wanting to try this recipe for ages but didnt have the right ingredients so I subbed rice for quinoa, walnuts for pecans, soy sauce for coconut aminos and ommited the salt. They were still absolutely delicious! My husband has only just started eating a plant based diet so any recipe that gets his approval is staying! The 2 1/2 tsp chili powder did make for a fiery burger but we really enjoyed it!<br/>
I made them up the night before, cooked them for lunch the following day and they were great. Nice to know I can pre prep for bbqs or quick meals. Perfect ?</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Everything was amazing! We don’t usually have pecans on hand so I just use whatever nut we have so I’ve used almonds and cashews, still turned out amazing! We have also made a bunch and instead of cooking them right away froze them and they were still amazing when we ate them later, just fried and cooked as the reciepe indicates. They are so delicious and definitely added to the weekly meal plans!</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-812099">
<article id="article-comment-812099">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Kay M." class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/82fb96096074b0c28d6a5156544bc2cc?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/82fb96096074b0c28d6a5156544bc2cc?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Kay M." width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Kay M.</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421785#comment-812099">July 5, 2019 at 9:42 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This was an awesome recipe! I added 1/2 quinoa and 1/2 brown rice. I omitted the salt, as I’m watching my sodium intake, and didn’t miss it! The texture was amazing! I kept some pieces of the beans and nuts intact, which allowed the burger to have some nice crunchiness throughout. I was pleasantly surprised by how firm the patty was without being dry. Baking the black beans was a genius move! I thought the recipe called for too much of the cumin and the chili powder, but I was wrong – the seasoning along with the BBQ sauce added so much flavor. Thank you for a tremendous recipe! I look forward to trying your other veggie burger recipes soon.</p>
<div class="wprm-comment-rating">

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421785#comment-784861">February 5, 2019 at 9:24 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Thanks for the reply but that is an article about calorie counting and I’m not sure if you understood my original comment. For this recipe, the macronutrients don’t add up to the calories. So either the calories or the macros are wrong. It’s not a huge deal because I track them myself but I do use them as a guideline as to what the ratios for your recipes are. I know I’m probably in the small minority of readers who care about this stuff but, as the article you linked states, it is important to look at the nutritional info of the food you are eating.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Yes, yes, yes to your comments that they do not fall apart and have great flavor! I cooked the potatoes (steamed chunks)  and rice (used some in other dishes) a couple of days ago, so these came together pretty quickly. I can imagine doing all the steps in one evening took your whole night!</p>

<p>SO GOOD! I topped mine with sautéed mushrooms (leftover from the burgers), mashed avocado, and pickled red onions. </p>
<p>My meat-eating boyfriend said the texture was the “meatiest” out of all of the veggie burgers I’ve ever made. We like thinner burgers so we ended up getting 8 out of the recipe &amp; paired it with sweet potato fries.</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421785#comment-758503">July 13, 2018 at 10:23 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Just finished making these! Haven’t tasted yet (lol) but they look awesome. I don’t have a food processor so I used my blender… if using a blender, I recommend blending beans + pecans/sweet potatoes + mushrooms and putting them in a separate bowl and then combinging together. It will help avoid the beans and pecans from becoming a purée while the potatoes stay whole. Thanks for the recipe!</p>
</div>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>These were excellent!  Loved the flavor and consistency.  Made a double batch and was able to get 10 burgers out of it.   Does require several steps but so worth it.  Unlike many other veggie burgers I’ve tried I had no issue with them falling apart.  I really think getting those beans super dry is the reason — so smart!     So we made 2 as directed and I’ve now frozen 8 pre frying/baking.   I’m serving them on Friday at my bday BBQ dinner.  I’ve read all the comments and still a bit confused as to the best strategy for cooking them out of the freezer — if it’s bake for 10 min then fry, for 8-10 min when does the BBQ sauce on top make an appearance.  Thanks so much!  Can’t wait to serve to my omni friends, along with your macaroni salad. :-)</p>

<p>Last night I made this for me and my partner. We subbed extra black beans because he doesn’t like quinoa. I didn’t have any vegan bbq sauce, so I just used the Hunts or whatever it was in my fridge. The burgers were a perfect consistency after briefly frying in a pan and then baking. We had them on potato rolls with tomato, onion, cheese, and pickles. My predominately carnivorous partner said he would totally eat them again. Good amount of prep work and dishes involved, but a fun date night in.</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>These burgers are the bomb!  I made them true to the recipe and it was very satisfying.  However next time I wanted to serve them on a bed of lettuce and thought to omit the BBQ sauce and use liquid smoke instead. Check!  Also for the dressing I processed avocado, jalapeno, lime juice and cilantro in the cuisinart.   This worked well on the burger and as a dressing for the salad which included raw veggie sticks and more of the roasted pecans.  Love this and so did the guests!  Thank you so much Dana for the great recipes!!  XOXO</p>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-753398">
<article id="article-comment-753398">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Kerstin" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a106e2fa68d71b3974944be2967e7ec5?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/a106e2fa68d71b3974944be2967e7ec5?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Kerstin" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Kerstin</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421785#comment-753398">May 22, 2018 at 2:49 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Delicious! So this is the most time consuming recipe I prepared for a while but it is worth it. I didn’t have any pecans so I used a mix between walnuts and sunflower seeds. Since I made this for the whole family (including a 3 and a 1-y-o) I used less BBQ sauce and added a bit of homemade ketchup instead and omitted the chili powder. My 3-y-o daughter was happy to help – she loves pushing the buttons of the food processor and making the patties. I cooked them only in the pan and they held together beautifully. Enough so that my 1-y-o son did not smash his patty. Since it does take a fair while I made double the amount so we can eat them again later on in the week.</p>

<li class="comment odd alt thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-753087">
<article id="article-comment-753087">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Kimberly" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/4f420aa063361af802f7e0dd49e5c9cb?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/4f420aa063361af802f7e0dd49e5c9cb?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Kimberly" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Kimberly</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421785#comment-753087">May 18, 2018 at 1:45 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I am an omnivore, but I often make plant based meals for my family to diversify our paletes. This was absolutely the best black bean burger I’ve ever made. The texture and flavor is just great. All 5 of my omni crew happily tucked in these burgers. I will definitely make these again.<br/>
I have seen comments about the mushrooms. If you don’t leave any visible chunks, or let a mushroom hater watch you add them in, I really don’t think the mushrooms will be noticeable. I have two mushroom haters in my crew and they didn’t bat an eye.</p>
<div class="wprm-comment-rating">

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-750374">
<article id="article-comment-750374">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Sarah Randall" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d8d2d9a4b225064e784499b1d404a410?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d8d2d9a4b225064e784499b1d404a410?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Sarah Randall" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Sarah Randall</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421785#comment-750374">April 22, 2018 at 1:15 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Best veggie burger!!! I love the strong barbecue flavor, how it is crispy on the outside and soft on the inside, and that it’s totally free of soy or other fillers. The finished product makes the prep time so worth it! I recommend serving with carmalized red onion.</p>
<p>We didn’t have mushrooms so we used peeled zucchini instead- worked perfectly! Do yourself a favor and make a double batch and freeze patties for an easy + quick dinner another night!</p>
<div class="wprm-comment-rating">

<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for LaLa" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/6e6aeeff713dc3d71fee30ce22875aa0?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/6e6aeeff713dc3d71fee30ce22875aa0?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for LaLa" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">LaLa</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421785#comment-749753">April 16, 2018 at 8:21 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>We have made many of your recipes over the past several years, but never left any comments. This recipe was SO good, i just had to let you know! As a Midwestern carnivore married to a vegan, this was my first attempt at making a veggie burger at home. We chose your recipe because the ingredients sounded so delicious and simple…and they were! These burgers turned out better than most veggie burgers I’ve tried (and loved) in restaurants.  The flavor and texture were PERFECT, so the long prep time was totally worth it. We followed your suggestion to use hemp seeds in place of pecans to make this recipe nut-free. I was impressed at how well the burgers held together and how crispy they were on the outside after baking. So glad we made a double batch!</p>
</div>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421785#comment-750489">April 23, 2018 at 9:06 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>A lil update on my above comment. I did freeze half the recipe when I made these after the refrigeration step. Once I thawed them, I panned fried them and put them in the oven like the recipe says. They were definitely more dry and crumbled apart a lil in the pan when frying. They were still good, but a lil to dry for my liking. Definitely best eaten right fresh.</p>
</div>

<p>These burgers tasted great, but never firmed  up. I don’t own a metal pan, so I water “fried” them in a ceramic coated skillet then baked them on a foil-lined baking sheet. Could that have affected the texture? Also, the patties were in the fridge for a few days before I actually cooked them. I don’t know if that had any impact. I’ll have to try again, making them thinner in the hopes that they’ll dry out more.</p>

<li class="comment even thread-odd thread-alt depth-1 wpr_madethis_li" id="comment-747756">
<article id="article-comment-747756">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Zoë" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9ab8a19efd67f8e7caf89ecb32405f4c?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9ab8a19efd67f8e7caf89ecb32405f4c?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Zoë" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Zoë</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421786#comment-747756">March 26, 2018 at 8:24 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I made these burgers tonight but they turned out super mushy! I was disappointed but it may have been my own mistake. The recipe also made 9 huge patties somehow. I cooked the beans just as you instructed. They were super dry but I steamed the yam. They were still al dente when I threw them in the food processor but could that have caused the mush? I guess I should’ve thrown in another dry ingredient but I was too hungry to play with the recipe so I baked them for a really long time to dry them out as much as possible. I’m gluten free and the buns I used were a bit stiff so with every bite the patty just squished out everywhere :( The flavour was delicious and I’ve made a lot of your recipes and they are fantastic. I’m convinced I did something wrong. I’ll definitely have to make this again but I’ll most likely crumble the remaining patties and use them as taco filling. I’m going to try the vanilla cake tomorrow :)</p>

<img alt="Avatar for Deirdre Richardson" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d54faacbfdf10fd1d6be46108615786e?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d54faacbfdf10fd1d6be46108615786e?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Deirdre Richardson" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Deirdre Richardson</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>WOW!  I have to say that I have never posted a comment before but these were so good, I had to.<br/>
I substituted cashews for the pecans due to my sons allergy to pecans.  I used Braggs liquid aminos instead of the coconut aminos (thats what I had in).  I also cut back a little on the chili powder and cumin. Other than that, I followed the recipe as written. They are moist (but not too), very flavorful and satisfying.  I used the pressing in the half cup method for shaping and it made 7 good sized patties.<br/>
I will definitely be making these again. </p>
<p>Thanks so much for all your great recipies!<br/>
Deirdre</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Just made these. They taste amazing, but they fell apart! The texture seemed perfect when I formed them. I followed all the cooking instructions and they held together for the most part when I placed them on a bun, however as soon as you started eating them they just crumbled. Any suggestions? I would love to be able to serve these to guests.</p>

<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Amy" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/0440ad340341cf5d47319500c671a9f2?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/0440ad340341cf5d47319500c671a9f2?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Amy" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Amy</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421786#comment-747425">March 23, 2018 at 3:59 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Wow! These look delicious- can’t wait to try. Reading through the instructions however it seems like there’s a lot of steps. After chilling the “dough” is it necessary to fry them for 10 minutes before baking them for another 10-15? Or could you just go straight from the fridge to the oven? Just trying to find ways to cut down on prep time.</p>
<p>Also  – do they freeze well &amp; do you freeze them before frying? Or before baking?</p>
<p>Thanks!</p>
</div>
<div class="comment-reply"><a aria-label="Reply to Amy" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-747425" data-commentid="747425" data-postid="30802" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-747425" rel="nofollow">Reply</a></div>

<ul class="children">
<li class="comment byuser comment-author-support even depth-2" id="comment-747433">
<article id="article-comment-747433">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Support @ Minimalist Baker" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9501d522e8b6b56b741d5c9b17c76182?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9501d522e8b6b56b741d5c9b17c76182?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Support @ Minimalist Baker" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Support @ Minimalist Baker</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421786#comment-747433">March 23, 2018 at 7:42 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Hi Amy! It’s best to sear both sides on the stovetop and then finish baking in the oven, where they will dry out and firm up a bit, but if you try cutting down steps, just know that they may not be as firm. As for freezing them, I recommend freezing prior to frying, and then when ready to use, bake them to thaw, followed by frying. Hope this helps!</p>
</div>
<div class="comment-reply"><a aria-label="Reply to Support @ Minimalist Baker" class="comment-reply-link" data-belowelement="comment-747433" data-commentid="747433" data-postid="30802" data-respondelement="respond" href="#comment-747433" rel="nofollow">Reply</a></div>

<p>These looked so good that I had to try it! I did sub out some ingredients that I didn’t have on hand though. I used regular potatoes, brown rice, and hemp seeds for the sweet potatoes, quinoa and pecans. </p>
<p>The flavors were delicious! Drying the black beans out in the oven really helped the texture a lot to prevent it from being overly mushy.</p>
<p>Thank you for a great recipe. My meat loving boyfriend scarfed down two :P</p>

<p>Well I just learned something!  Apparently I’ve been cooking mushrooms all wrong; loved the way these turned out.  Keeping it healthy I made a super simple BBQ sauce and after frying the burgers I put them in the oven on the cookie sheet with parchment paper and then wilted some greens in the fry pan.  Very Nice Indeed.</p>

<p>This was absolutely delicious. We had this yesterday with red cabbage and caramelized balsamic red onions. I wonder though, if I could do something about the crumbly texture. While raw, the consistency was really dough-like and easy to press into patties, but after baking it it held its form but crumbled quite a lot while eating.  Maybe my patties were too thin? They were about the size and thickness of the palm of my hand. I will absolutely make this again, thank you so much for sharing !</p>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1" id="comment-747159">
<article id="article-comment-747159">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for Katie" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/4fff553f676de6981b1c1db672ef7f0d?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/4fff553f676de6981b1c1db672ef7f0d?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Katie" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">Katie</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421786#comment-747159">March 20, 2018 at 7:02 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Hi Dana,</p>
<p>I’ve tried the bake-beans-before-burgers trick and it’s fantastic! Who likes mushy burgers? Not me! I am a bit lazy sometimes though, and the process of soaking beans, cooking beans, then baking them is a lot of steps. I just tried a burger recipe treating the beans the way I do falafel, and I can’t figure out why I didn’t do it before: don’t cook the soaked beans, just rinse after soaking and throw in the processor! The beans turn into the same texture as pulsed nuts and cook wonderfully in the burger. Less steps :)</p>
<p>Cheers,<br/>
Katie<br/>
*Of course, this hack is for if you use dried beans. Canned beans and baking is definitely the way to go!</p>
</div>

<p>Hi Dana – Love your stuff !<br/>

Most of your vegan stuff has a high protein bean or nut which I fiddle with and take out or substitute but as you spend way more time in the creation phase than I do, I was just wondering if you could think up a low protein burger mix … as summer is coming here in Ohio !!!</p>
<p>Chris</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421786#comment-747245">March 21, 2018 at 10:38 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Hi Chris! These ones aren’t too high protein. But to make this lower protein, sub the quinoa for brown or white rice, increase the amount of grain you add, and cut the beans back. Hope that helps!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Just made this tonight and they were fantastic!  I followed the recipe with no substitutions.  The prep work does take some time but the burgers were worth it.  Due to my schedule that day, I did have to stick the burgers in the fridge after I pan fried them and before i put them in the oven with the barbecue sauce.  I just baked them a tad bit longer to make sure they were hot and browned.  Served them on thin buns with avocado, slaw, onion, pickle, lettuce, and red bell pepper slices.  So good!</p>

Definitely a keeper.</p>

<p>Hi Becca, I swap beans in recipes all the time. You can also try kidney beans as well. It does change the taste some but not much. You could also try cannellini beans or kidney beans mixed with cooked brown lentils. Looking foreward to making this recipe.<br/>
 Gina</p>

<p>I started making this and realized I was out of black beans (whoops!) so I subbed a can of pinto instead and it was delicious! May have had a bit more liquid compared to black but we enjoyed it. This is my favorite vegan burger-substitute!</p>

<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421786#comment-747234">March 21, 2018 at 10:29 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>One of the best home made BBQ sauces I’ve had in 45 years of being a be vegetarian is, with some modifications, the one in the 40 + year old:  THE FARM COOKBOOK, the BBQ sauce for Gluten ribs.  I use much less sweet, salt,  oil and mustard.  It is not hard to make, but does require a full hour of simmer time, which makes all the flavors transform and wonderful.  Check it out.  All in one big cast Iron pan.  Awesome!  Ann</p>
</div>

<li class="comment even thread-odd thread-alt depth-1" id="comment-746937">
<article id="article-comment-746937">
<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<img alt="Avatar for MIchelle" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9b9783875a2c5164032779222780aad0?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/9b9783875a2c5164032779222780aad0?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for MIchelle" width="96"/><span itemprop="name">MIchelle</span> <span class="says">says</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/smoky-bbq-black-bean-burger/?t=1582421786#comment-746937">March 18, 2018 at 5:34 pm</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Super easy to make your own BBQ sauce… This recipe from Isa is a go to for me. I make a extra, and place it in tiny tupperwares in the freezer.</p>
<p>For the BBQ Sauce:<br/>
1/2 cup vegetable broth<br/>
2 tablespoons pure maple syrup<br/>
2 tablespoons molasses<br/>
2 tablespoons tomato paste<br/>
2 tablespoons peanut butter<br/>
1 tablespoon soy sauce (I sub coconut aminos)<br/>
1 tablespoon apple cider vinegar<br/>
1 tablespoon prepared mustard (I use Dijon)<br/>
1/2 teaspoon liquid smoke<br/>
1/2 teaspoon Sriracha hot sauce</p>
</div>

				jQuery(document).ready(function () {

					function mgclInit() {
						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.no-lightbox').click(mgclOnClick);

						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('a.set-target').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('a.set-target').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.set-target').click(mgclOnClick);
					}

					function mgclOnClick() {
						if (!this.target || this.target == '' || this.target == '_self')
							window.location = this.href;
						else
							window.open(this.href,this.target);
						return false;
					}

					// From WP Gallery Custom Links
					// Reduce the number of  conflicting lightboxes
					function mgclAddLoadEvent(func) {
						var oldOnload = window.onload;
						if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
							window.onload = func;
						} else {
							window.onload = function() {
								oldOnload();
								func();
							}
						}
					}

					mgclAddLoadEvent(mgclInit);
					mgclInit();

				});
